<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Output-Customization">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Grouping-Options" accesskey="n" rel="next">Grouping Options</a>, Previous: <a href="#Error-Checking-and-Calculation-Options" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Error Checking and Calculation Options</a>, Up: <a href="#Command_002dLine-Quick-Reference" accesskey="u" rel="up">Command-Line Quick Reference</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Output-Customization-1">8.2.5 Output Customization</h4>

<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcollapse'><span><samp class="option">--collapse</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcollapse'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dn'><span><samp class="option">-n</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dn'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Collapse transactions with multiple postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsubtotal-2'><span><samp class="option">--subtotal</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsubtotal-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002ds'><span><samp class="option">-s</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002ds'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report register as a single subtotal.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dby_002dpayee-2'><span><samp class="option">--by-payee</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dby_002dpayee-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dP'><span><samp class="option">-P</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dP'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report subtotals by payee.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dempty-1'><span><samp class="option">--empty</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dempty-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dE'><span><samp class="option">-E</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dE'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Include empty accounts in the report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dweekly'><span><samp class="option">--weekly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dweekly'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dW'><span><samp class="option">-W</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dW'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals by week.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dquarterly'><span><samp class="option">--quarterly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dquarterly'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals by quarter.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dyearly'><span><samp class="option">--yearly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dyearly'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dY'><span><samp class="option">-Y</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dY'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals by year.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddow'><span><samp class="option">--dow</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddow'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals by day of week.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsort-VEXPR'><span><samp class="option">--sort <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsort-VEXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dS-VEXPR'><span><samp class="option">-S <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dS-VEXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Sort a report using <var class="var">VEXPR</var>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dwide'><span><samp class="option">--wide</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dwide'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dw'><span><samp class="option">-w</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dw'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Assume 132 columns instead of 80.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dhead-INT'><span><samp class="option">--head <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dhead-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the first <var class="var">INT</var> postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtail-INT'><span><samp class="option">--tail <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtail-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the last <var class="var">INT</var> postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpager-FILE'><span><samp class="option">--pager <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpager-FILE'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Direct output to <var class="var">FILE</var> pager program.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002dpager'><span><samp class="option">--no-pager</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002dpager'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Direct output to stdout, avoiding pager program.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daverage-1'><span><samp class="option">--average</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daverage-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dA'><span><samp class="option">-A</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dA'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the average posting value.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddeviation'><span><samp class="option">--deviation</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddeviation'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dD'><span><samp class="option">-D</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dD'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report each posting&rsquo;s deviation from the average.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpercent'><span><samp class="option">--percent</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpercent'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_0025'><span><samp class="option">-%</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_0025'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show subtotals in the balance report as percentages.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpivot-TAG'><span><samp class="option">--pivot <var class="var">TAG</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpivot-TAG'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Produce a pivot table of the <var class="var">TAG</var> type specified.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002damount_002ddata-2'><span><samp class="option">--amount-data</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002damount_002ddata-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dj'><span><samp class="option">-j</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dj'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show only the date and value columns to format the output for plots.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dplot_002damount_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--plot-amount-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dplot_002damount_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format for the plot output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtotal_002ddata-2'><span><samp class="option">--total-data</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtotal_002ddata-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dJ'><span><samp class="option">-J</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dJ'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show only the date and total columns to format the output for plots.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dplot_002dtotal_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--plot-total-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dplot_002dtotal_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format for the plot output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddisplay-EXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">--display <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddisplay-EXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dd-EXPR'><span><samp class="option">-d <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dd-EXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display only postings that meet the criteria in the <var class="var">EXPR</var>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT'><span><samp class="option">--date-format <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dy-DATE_005fFORMAT'><span><samp class="option">-y <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dy-DATE_005fFORMAT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Change the basic date format used in reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbalance_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--balance-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbalance_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dregister_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--register-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dregister_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprices_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--prices-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprices_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dF-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">-F <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dF-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the reporting format for various reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002danon'><span><samp class="option">--anon</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002danon'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Print the ledger register with anonymized accounts and payees, useful
for filing bug reports.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>

<dl class="ftable">

</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddaily'><span><samp class="option">--daily</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddaily'> &para;</a></span></dt>

</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dweekly-1'><span><samp class="option">--weekly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dweekly-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dW-1'><span><samp class="option">-W</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dW-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>

</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmonthly-2'><span><samp class="option">--monthly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmonthly-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dM'><span><samp class="option">-M</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dM'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Group postings by month.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dquarterly-1'><span><samp class="option">--quarterly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dquarterly-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>

</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dyearly-1'><span><samp class="option">--yearly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dyearly-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dY-1'><span><samp class="option">-Y</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dY-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Group postings by year.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddow-1'><span><samp class="option">--dow</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddow-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Group by day of weeks.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsubtotal-3'><span><samp class="option">--subtotal</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsubtotal-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002ds-1'><span><samp class="option">-s</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002ds-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Group postings together, similar to the balance report.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<h4 class="subsection" id="Commodity-Reporting-1">8.2.7 Commodity Reporting</h4>

<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprice_002ddb-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">--price-db <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprice_002ddb-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>

</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprice_002dexp-INT'><span><samp class="option">--price-exp <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprice_002dexp-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dleeway-INT'><span><samp class="option">--leeway <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dleeway-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dZ-INT'><span><samp class="option">-Z <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dZ-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set expected freshness of prices in <var class="var">INT</var> minutes.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddownload-1'><span><samp class="option">--download</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddownload-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dQ'><span><samp class="option">-Q</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dQ'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Download quotes using the script named <samp class="file">getquote</samp>.
</p>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dquantity'><span><samp class="option">--quantity</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dquantity'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dO'><span><samp class="option">-O</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dO'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report commodity totals without conversion.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbasis'><span><samp class="option">--basis</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbasis'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dB'><span><samp class="option">-B</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dB'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report cost basis.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmarket-3'><span><samp class="option">--market</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmarket-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dV'><span><samp class="option">-V</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dV'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report last known market value.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dgain'><span><samp class="option">--gain</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dgain'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dG'><span><samp class="option">-G</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dG'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report net gain or loss for commodities that have a price history.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<div class="section-level-extent" id="Detailed-Option-Description">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Period-Expressions" accesskey="n" rel="next">Period Expressions</a>, Previous: <a href="#Command_002dLine-Quick-Reference" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Command-Line Quick Reference</a>, Up: <a href="#Command_002dLine-Syntax" accesskey="u" rel="up">Command-Line Syntax</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h3 class="section" id="Detailed-Option-Description-1">8.3 Detailed Option Description</h3>


<ul class="mini-toc">
<li><a href="#Global-Options" accesskey="1">Global Options</a></li>
<li><a href="#Session-Options" accesskey="2">Session Options</a></li>
<li><a href="#Report-Options" accesskey="3">Report Options</a></li>
<li><a href="#Basic-options" accesskey="4">Basic options</a></li>
<li><a href="#Report-filtering" accesskey="5">Report filtering</a></li>
<li><a href="#Output-customization" accesskey="6">Output customization</a></li>
<li><a href="#Commodity-reporting" accesskey="7">Commodity reporting</a></li>
<li><a href="#Environment-variables" accesskey="8">Environment variables</a></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Global-Options">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Session-Options" accesskey="n" rel="next">Session Options</a>, Previous: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Detailed Option Description</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Global-Options-1">8.3.1 Global Options</h4>

<p>Options for Ledger reports affect three separate scopes of operation:
Global, Session, and Report.  In practice there is very little
difference between these scopes.  Ledger 3.0 contains provisions for
GUIs, which would make use of the different scopes by keeping an
instance of Ledger running in the background and running multiple
sessions with multiple reports per session.
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dargs_002donly'><span><samp class="option">--args-only</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dargs_002donly'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Ignore all environment and init-file settings and
use only command-line arguments to control Ledger.  Useful for debugging
or testing small journal files not associated with your main financial
database.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddebug-CODE'><span><samp class="option">--debug <var class="var">CODE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddebug-CODE'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p><small class="sc">UNDOCUMENTED</small>! Please help by contributing documentation for this feature.
If ledger has been built with debug options this will provide extra data during
the run.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dhelp-1'><span><samp class="option">--help</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dhelp-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dh-1'><span><samp class="option">-h</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dh-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display the man page for <samp class="file">ledger</samp>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dinit_002dfile-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">--init-file <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dinit_002dfile-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the location of the init file.  By default, <samp class="file">$XDG_CONFIG_HOME</samp>,
<samp class="file">~/.config/ledger/ledgerrc</samp>, <samp class="file">~/.ledgerrc</samp> and <samp class="file">./.ledgerrc</samp> are
tried in order.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002doptions'><span><samp class="option">--options</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002doptions'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display the options in effect for this Ledger invocation, along with
their values and the source of those values, for example:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger --options bal --cleared
</pre></div>

<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">===============================================================================
[Global scope options]
             --args-only                                             --args-only

[Session scope options]
                  --file = A9349E4.dat                               --file

[Report scope options]
               --cleared                                             --cleared
               --columns = 80                                        --columns
                 --limit = cleared                                   --cleared
===============================================================================
              $15.00  Expenses
              $12.45    Food
               $2.55    Tips
             $-15.00  Liabilities:MasterCard
--------------------
                   0
</pre></div>

<p>For the source column, a value starting with a &lsquo;<samp class="samp">-</samp>&rsquo; or &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--</samp>&rsquo;
indicated the source was a command-line argument.  If the entry starts
with a &lsquo;<samp class="samp">$</samp>&rsquo;, the source was an environment variable.  If the source
is <code class="code">?normalize</code> the value was set internally by ledger, in
a function called <code class="code">normalize_options</code>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dscript-FILE'><span><samp class="option">--script <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dscript-FILE'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Execute a ledger script.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtrace-INT'><span><samp class="option">--trace <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtrace-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Enable tracing.  The <var class="var">INT</var> specifies the level of trace desired.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dverbose'><span><samp class="option">--verbose</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dverbose'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dv'><span><samp class="option">-v</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dv'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Print detailed information on the execution of Ledger.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dverify'><span><samp class="option">--verify</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dverify'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Enable additional assertions during run-time.  This causes a significant
slowdown.  When combined with <samp class="option">--debug <var class="var">CODE</var></samp> ledger will
produce memory trace information.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dverify_002dmemory'><span><samp class="option">--verify-memory</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dverify_002dmemory'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Verify that every constructed object is properly destructed.  This is for
debugging purposes only.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dversion-1'><span><samp class="option">--version</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dversion-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Print version information and exit.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Session-Options">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Report-Options" accesskey="n" rel="next">Report Options</a>, Previous: <a href="#Global-Options" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Global Options</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Session-Options-1">8.3.2 Session Options</h4>

<p>Options for Ledger reports affect three separate scopes of operation:
Global, Session, and Report.  In practice there is very little
difference between these scopes.  Ledger 3.0 contains provisions for
GUIs, which would make use of the different scopes by keeping an
instance of Ledger running in the background and running multiple
sessions with multiple reports per session.
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcheck_002dpayees-1'><span><samp class="option">--check-payees</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcheck_002dpayees-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Enable strict and pedantic checking for payees as well as accounts,
commodities and tags.  This only works in conjunction with
<samp class="option">--strict</samp> or <samp class="option">--pedantic</samp>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dday_002dbreak'><span><samp class="option">--day-break</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dday_002dbreak'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Break up <code class="command">register</code> report of <a class="ref" href="#timelog">timelog</a> entries that span multiple
days by day.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddecimal_002dcomma'><span><samp class="option">--decimal-comma</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddecimal_002dcomma'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Direct Ledger to parse journals using the European standard comma as
a decimal separator, not the usual period.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddownload-2'><span><samp class="option">--download</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddownload-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dQ-1'><span><samp class="option">-Q</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dQ-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Direct Ledger to download prices.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dfile-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">--file <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dfile-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002df-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">-f <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002df-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the input <samp class="file">FILE</samp> for this invocation.
</p>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dinput_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT-1'><span><samp class="option">--input-date-format <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dinput_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the input date format for journal entries.  For example,
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger convert Export.csv --input-date-format &quot;%m/%d/%Y&quot;
</pre></div>

<p>Would convert the <samp class="file">Export.csv</samp> file to ledger format, assuming
the dates in the CSV file are like 12/23/2009 (see <a class="pxref" href="#Date-and-Time-Format-Codes">Date and Time Format Codes</a>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmaster_002daccount-STR'><span><samp class="option">--master-account <var class="var">STR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmaster_002daccount-STR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Prepend all account names with the argument.
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -f drewr3.dat bal --no-total --master-account HUMBUG
</pre></div>

<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">                   0  HUMBUG
         $ -3,804.00    Assets
          $ 1,396.00      Checking
             $ 30.00        Business
         $ -5,200.00      Savings
         $ -1,000.00    Equity:Opening Balances
          $ 6,654.00    Expenses
          $ 5,500.00      Auto
             $ 20.00      Books
            $ 300.00      Escrow
            $ 334.00      Food:Groceries
            $ 500.00      Interest:Mortgage
         $ -2,030.00    Income
         $ -2,000.00      Salary
            $ -30.00      Sales
            $ 180.00    Liabilities
            $ -20.00      MasterCard
            $ 200.00      Mortgage:Principal
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002daliases'><span><samp class="option">--no-aliases</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002daliases'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Ledger does not expand any aliases if this option is specified.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpedantic-2'><span><samp class="option">--pedantic</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpedantic-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Accounts, tags or commodities not previously declared will cause errors.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpermissive-1'><span><samp class="option">--permissive</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpermissive-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Quiet balance assertions.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprice_002ddb-FILE-2'><span><samp class="option">--price-db <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprice_002ddb-FILE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the location of the price entry data file.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprice_002dexp-INT-1'><span><samp class="option">--price-exp <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprice_002dexp-INT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dleeway-INT-1'><span><samp class="option">--leeway <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dleeway-INT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dZ-INT-1'><span><samp class="option">-Z <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dZ-INT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the expected freshness of price quotes, in <var class="var">INT</var> minutes.  That
is, if the last known quote for any commodity is older than this value,
and if <samp class="option">--download</samp> is being used, then the Internet will be
consulted again for a newer price.  Otherwise, the old price is still
considered to be fresh enough.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dstrict-3'><span><samp class="option">--strict</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dstrict-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Ledger normally silently accepts any account or commodity in a posting,
even if you have misspelled a commonly used one.  The option
<samp class="option">--strict</samp> changes that behavior.  While running with
<samp class="option">--strict</samp>, Ledger interprets all cleared transactions as
correct, and if it encounters a new account or commodity (same as
a misspelled commodity or account) it will issue a warning giving you
the file and line number of the problem.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002drecursive_002daliases'><span><samp class="option">--recursive-aliases</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drecursive_002daliases'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Normally, ledger only expands aliases once.  With this option, ledger
tries to expand the result of alias expansion recursively, until no more
expansions apply.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtime_002dcolon'><span><samp class="option">--time-colon</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtime_002dcolon'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>The <samp class="option">--time-colon</samp> option will display the value for a seconds
based commodity as real hours and minutes.
</p>
<p>For example 8100 seconds by default will be displayed as 2.25 whereas
with the <samp class="option">--time-colon</samp> option they will be displayed as 2:15.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dvalue_002dexpr-VEXPR'><span><samp class="option">--value-expr <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dvalue_002dexpr-VEXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set a global value expression annotation.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Report-Options">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Basic-options" accesskey="n" rel="next">Basic options</a>, Previous: <a href="#Session-Options" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Session Options</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Report-Options-1">8.3.3 Report Options</h4>

<p>Options for Ledger reports affect three separate scopes of operation:
Global, Session, and Report.  In practice there is very little
difference between these scopes.  Ledger 3.0 contains provisions for
GUIs, which would make use of the different scopes by keeping an
instance of Ledger running in the background and running multiple
sessions with multiple reports per session.
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dabbrev_002dlen-INT'><span><samp class="option">--abbrev-len <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dabbrev_002dlen-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the minimum length an account can be abbreviated to if it doesn&rsquo;t
fit inside the <code class="code">account-width</code>.  If <var class="var">INT</var> is zero, then the
account name will be truncated on the right.  If <var class="var">INT</var> is greater
than <code class="code">account-width</code> then the account will be truncated on the
left, with no shortening of the account names in order to fit into the
desired width.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daccount-STR-2'><span><samp class="option">--account <var class="var">STR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daccount-STR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Prepend <var class="var">STR</var> to all accounts reported.  That is, the option
&lsquo;<samp class="samp">--account Personal</samp>&rsquo; would tack &lsquo;<samp class="samp">Personal:</samp>&rsquo; to the beginning
of every account reported in a balance report or register report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daccount_002dwidth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--account-width <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daccount_002dwidth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the width of the account column in the <code class="command">register</code> report
to <var class="var">INT</var> characters.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dactual-1'><span><samp class="option">--actual</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dactual-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dL-1'><span><samp class="option">-L</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dL-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report only real transactions, ignoring all automated or virtual
transactions.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dadd_002dbudget-1'><span><samp class="option">--add-budget</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dadd_002dbudget-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show only unbudgeted postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002damount-EXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">--amount <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002damount-EXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dt-EXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">-t <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dt-EXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Apply the given value expression to the posting amount (see <a class="pxref" href="#Value-Expressions">Value Expressions</a>).  Using <samp class="option">--amount <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp> you can apply an
arbitrary transformation to the postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002damount_002ddata-3'><span><samp class="option">--amount-data</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002damount_002ddata-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dj-1'><span><samp class="option">-j</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dj-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>On a register report print only the date and amount of postings.
Useful for graphing and spreadsheet applications.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002damount_002dwidth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--amount-width <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002damount_002dwidth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the width in characters of the amount column in the
<code class="command">register</code> report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002danon-1'><span><samp class="option">--anon</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002danon-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Anonymize registry output, mostly for sending in bug reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dauto_002dmatch-1'><span><samp class="option">--auto-match</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dauto_002dmatch-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>When generating a ledger transaction from a CSV file using the
<code class="command">convert</code> command, automatically match an account from the
Ledger journal.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daux_002ddate-1'><span><samp class="option">--aux-date</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daux_002ddate-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002deffective-1'><span><samp class="option">--effective</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002deffective-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show auxiliary dates for all calculations (see <a class="pxref" href="#Effective-Dates">Effective Dates</a>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daverage-2'><span><samp class="option">--average</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daverage-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dA-1'><span><samp class="option">-A</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dA-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Print average values over the number of transactions instead of
running totals.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daverage_002dlot_002dprices'><span><samp class="option">--average-lot-prices</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daverage_002dlot_002dprices'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the average price at which each commodity was purchased in
a balance report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbalance_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--balance-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbalance_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format to use for the <code class="command">balance</code> report (see <a class="pxref" href="#Format-Strings">Format Strings</a>).  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(justify(scrub(display_total), 20, -1, true, color))&quot;
&quot;  %(!options.flat ? depth_spacer : \&quot;\&quot;)&quot;
&quot;%-(ansify_if(partial_account(options.flat), blue if color))\n%/&quot;
&quot;%$1\n%/&quot;
&quot;--------------------\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbase'><span><samp class="option">--base</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbase'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Reduce convertible commodities down the bottom of the conversion, e.g.
display time in seconds.  This also applies to custom commodity
conversions (see <a class="pxref" href="#Commodity-equivalences">Commodity equivalences</a>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbasis-1'><span><samp class="option">--basis</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbasis-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dB-1'><span><samp class="option">-B</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dB-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcost'><span><samp class="option">--cost</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcost'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the cost basis on all posting.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbegin-DATE-1'><span><samp class="option">--begin <var class="var">DATE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbegin-DATE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the start <var class="var">DATE</var> of all calculations.  Transactions before
that date will be ignored.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbold_002dif-VEXPR'><span><samp class="option">--bold-if <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbold_002dif-VEXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Print the entire line in bold if the given value expression is true
(see <a class="pxref" href="#Value-Expressions">Value Expressions</a>).
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger reg Expenses --begin Dec --bold-if &quot;amount&gt;100&quot;
</pre></div>

<p>list all transactions since the beginning of December and print in
bold any posting greater than $100.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbudget-2'><span><samp class="option">--budget</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbudget-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Only display budgeted items.  In a register report this
displays transactions in the budget, in a balance report this displays
accounts in the budget (see <a class="pxref" href="#Budgeting-and-Forecasting">Budgeting and Forecasting</a>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbudget_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--budget-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbudget_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format to use for the <code class="command">budget</code> report (see <a class="pxref" href="#Format-Strings">Format Strings</a>).  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(justify(scrub(get_at(display_total, 0)), 12, -1, true, color))&quot;
&quot; %(justify(-scrub(get_at(display_total, 1)), 12, &quot;
&quot;           12 + 1 + 12, true, color))&quot;
&quot; %(justify(scrub(get_at(display_total, 1) + &quot;
&quot;                 get_at(display_total, 0)), 12, &quot;
&quot;           12 + 1 + 12 + 1 + 12, true, color))&quot;
&quot; %(ansify_if(&quot;
&quot;   justify((get_at(display_total, 1) ? &quot;
&quot;            (100% * quantity(scrub(get_at(display_total, 0)))) / &quot;
&quot;             -quantity(scrub(get_at(display_total, 1))) : 0), &quot;
&quot;           5, -1, true, false),&quot;
&quot;   magenta if (color and get_at(display_total, 1) and &quot;
&quot;               (abs(quantity(scrub(get_at(display_total, 0))) / &quot;
&quot;                    quantity(scrub(get_at(display_total, 1)))) &gt;= 1))))&quot;
&quot;  %(!options.flat ? depth_spacer : \&quot;\&quot;)&quot;
&quot;%-(ansify_if(partial_account(options.flat), blue if color))\n&quot;
&quot;%/%$1 %$2 %$3 %$4\n%/&quot;
&quot;%(prepend_width ? \&quot; \&quot; * int(prepend_width) : \&quot;\&quot;)&quot;
&quot;------------ ------------ ------------ -----\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dby_002dpayee-4'><span><samp class="option">--by-payee</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dby_002dpayee-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dP-2'><span><samp class="option">-P</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dP-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Group the register report by payee.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcleared-2'><span><samp class="option">--cleared</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcleared-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dC-1'><span><samp class="option">-C</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dC-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Consider only transactions that have been cleared for display and
calculation.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcleared_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--cleared-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcleared_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format to use for the <code class="command">cleared</code> report (see <a class="pxref" href="#Format-Strings">Format Strings</a>).  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(justify(scrub(get_at(total_expr, 0)), 16, 16 + prepend_width, &quot;
&quot; true, color))  %(justify(scrub(get_at(total_expr, 1)), 18, &quot;
&quot; 36 + prepend_width, true, color))&quot;
&quot;    %(latest_cleared ? format_date(latest_cleared) : \&quot;         \&quot;)&quot;
&quot;    %(!options.flat ? depth_spacer : \&quot;\&quot;)&quot;
&quot;%-(ansify_if(partial_account(options.flat), blue if color))\n%/&quot;
&quot;%$1  %$2    %$3\n%/&quot;
&quot;%(prepend_width ? \&quot; \&quot; * prepend_width : \&quot;\&quot;)&quot;
&quot;----------------    ----------------    ---------\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcollapse-1'><span><samp class="option">--collapse</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcollapse-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dn-1'><span><samp class="option">-n</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dn-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>By default ledger prints all accounts in an account tree.  With
<samp class="option">--collapse</samp> it prints only the top level account specified.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcollapse_002dif_002dzero'><span><samp class="option">--collapse-if-zero</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcollapse_002dif_002dzero'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Collapse the account display only if it has a zero balance.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcolor'><span><samp class="option">--color</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcolor'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dansi'><span><samp class="option">--ansi</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dansi'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use color if the terminal supports it.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcolumns-INT'><span><samp class="option">--columns <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcolumns-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the width of the <code class="command">register</code> report in characters.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcount-1'><span><samp class="option">--count</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcount-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Direct ledger to report the number of items when appended to the
<code class="command">commodities</code>, <code class="command">accounts</code> or <code class="command">payees</code> command.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcsv_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--csv-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcsv_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format to use for the <code class="command">csv</code> report (see <a class="pxref" href="#Format-Strings">Format Strings</a>).  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(quoted(date)),&quot;
&quot;%(quoted(code)),&quot;
&quot;%(quoted(payee)),&quot;
&quot;%(quoted(display_account)),&quot;
&quot;%(quoted(commodity(scrub(display_amount)))),&quot;
&quot;%(quoted(quantity(scrub(display_amount)))),&quot;
&quot;%(quoted(cleared ? \&quot;*\&quot; : (pending ? \&quot;!\&quot; : \&quot;\&quot;))),&quot;
&quot;%(quoted(join(note | xact.note)))\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcurrent-1'><span><samp class="option">--current</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcurrent-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Shorthand for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--limit &quot;date &lt;= today&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddaily-1'><span><samp class="option">--daily</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddaily-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dD-2'><span><samp class="option">-D</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dD-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Shorthand for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--period &quot;daily&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddate-EXPR'><span><samp class="option">--date <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddate-EXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Transform the date of the transaction using <var class="var">EXPR</var>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT-1'><span><samp class="option">--date-format <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dy-DATE_005fFORMAT-1'><span><samp class="option">-y <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dy-DATE_005fFORMAT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format ledger should use to read and print dates
(see <a class="pxref" href="#Date-and-Time-Format-Codes">Date and Time Format Codes</a>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddate_002dwidth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--date-width <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddate_002dwidth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the width, in characters, of the date column in the
<code class="command">register</code> report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddatetime_002dformat-DATETIME_005fFORMAT'><span><samp class="option">--datetime-format <var class="var">DATETIME_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddatetime_002dformat-DATETIME_005fFORMAT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the format ledger should use to print datetimes.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddc-1'><span><samp class="option">--dc</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddc-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display register or balance in debit/credit format If you use
<samp class="option">--dc</samp> with either the <code class="command">register</code> (reg) or
<code class="command">balance</code> (bal) commands, you will now get extra columns.
The register goes from this:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">12-Mar-10 Employer           Assets:Cash                $100        $100
                             Income:Employer           $-100           0
12-Mar-10 KFC                Expenses:Food               $20         $20
                             Assets:Cash                $-20           0
12-Mar-10 KFC - Rebate       Assets:Cash                  $5          $5
                             Expenses:Food               $-5           0
12-Mar-10 KFC - Food &amp; Reb.. Expenses:Food               $20         $20
                             Expenses:Food               $-5         $15
                             Assets:Cash                $-15           0
</pre></div>

<p>To this:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">12-Mar-10 Employer       Assets:Cash        $100           0        $100
                         In:Employer           0        $100           0
12-Mar-10 KFC            Expens:Food         $20           0         $20
                         Assets:Cash           0         $20           0
12-Mar-10 KFC - Rebate   Assets:Cash          $5           0          $5
                         Expens:Food           0          $5           0
12-Mar-10 KFC - Food &amp;.. Expens:Food         $20           0         $20
                         Expens:Food           0          $5         $15
                         Assets:Cash           0         $15           0
</pre></div>

<p>Where the first column is debits, the second is credits, and the third
is the running total.  Only the running total may contain negative
values.
</p>
<p>For the balance report without <samp class="option">--dc</samp>:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">                 $70  Assets:Cash
                 $30  Expenses:Food
               $-100  Income:Employer
--------------------
                   0
</pre></div>

<p>And with <samp class="option">--dc</samp> it becomes this:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">          $105            $35            $70  Assets:Cash
           $40            $10            $30  Expenses:Food
             0           $100          $-100  Income:Employer
--------------------------------------------
          $145           $145              0
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddepth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--depth <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddepth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Limit the depth of displayed accounts in balance and register reports.  Any
accounts of greater depth are folded into their parent at the specified level.
For example with &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--depth 2</samp>&rsquo; the account &lsquo;<samp class="samp">Expenses:Entertainment</samp>&rsquo;
would be folded into &lsquo;<samp class="samp">Expenses:Entertainment:Dining</samp>&rsquo; for display.
Importantly, this is a display predicate, which means it only
affects display, not the total calculations.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddeviation-1'><span><samp class="option">--deviation</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddeviation-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report each postingâs deviation from the average.  It is only meaningful
in the register and prices reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddisplay-EXPR-3'><span><samp class="option">--display <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddisplay-EXPR-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display only lines that satisfy the expression <var class="var">EXPR</var>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddisplay_002damount-EXPR'><span><samp class="option">--display-amount <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddisplay_002damount-EXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Apply a transformation to the <em class="emph">displayed</em> amount.  This happens
after calculations occur.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddisplay_002dtotal-EXPR'><span><samp class="option">--display-total <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddisplay_002dtotal-EXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Apply a transformation to the <em class="emph">displayed</em> total.  This happens after
calculations occur.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddow-2'><span><samp class="option">--dow</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddow-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddays_002dof_002dweek'><span><samp class="option">--days-of-week</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddays_002dof_002dweek'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Group transactions by the day of the week.
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger reg Expenses --dow --collapse
</pre></div>

<p>Will print all Expenses totaled for each day of the week.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dempty-2'><span><samp class="option">--empty</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dempty-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dE-1'><span><samp class="option">-E</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Include empty accounts in the report and in average calculations.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dend-DATE-1'><span><samp class="option">--end <var class="var">DATE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dend-DATE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the end <var class="var">DATE</var> for a transaction to be considered in the
report.  All transactions on or after this date are ignored.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dequity'><span><samp class="option">--equity</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dequity'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Related to the <code class="command">equity</code> command (see <a class="pxref" href="#The-equity-command">The <code class="command">equity</code> command</a>).  Gives current account balances in the form of a register
report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dexact'><span><samp class="option">--exact</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dexact'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report beginning and ending of periods by the date of the first and last
posting occurring in that period.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dexchange-_0022COMMODITY-_005b_002c-COMMODITY_002c-_002e_002e_002e_005d_0022-2'><span><samp class="option">--exchange &quot;<var class="var">COMMODITY</var> [, <var class="var">COMMODITY</var>, ...]&quot;</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dexchange-_0022COMMODITY-_005b_002c-COMMODITY_002c-_002e_002e_002e_005d_0022-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dX-_0022COMMODITY-_005b_002c-COMMODITY_002c-_002e_002e_002e_005d_0022'><span><samp class="option">-X &quot;<var class="var">COMMODITY</var> [, <var class="var">COMMODITY</var>, ...]&quot;</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dX-_0022COMMODITY-_005b_002c-COMMODITY_002c-_002e_002e_002e_005d_0022'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display values in terms of the given <var class="var">COMMODITY</var>.  If multiple
commodities are given, values in a listed commodity will remain as-is,
and others will be displayed in the first listed commodity they can be
converted to.
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger balance assets
</pre></div>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">             100 EUR
             100 PHP
             100 USD  Assets
             100 EUR    EUR Bank
             100 PHP    PHP Bank
             100 USD    USD Bank
--------------------
             100 EUR
             100 PHP
             100 USD
</pre></div>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger balance assets --exchange PHP
</pre></div>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">           11382 PHP  Assets
            5801 PHP    EUR Bank
             100 PHP    PHP Bank
            5481 PHP    USD Bank
--------------------
           11382 PHP
</pre></div>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger balance assets --exchange &quot;PHP, EUR&quot;
</pre></div>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">             100 EUR
            5581 PHP  Assets
             100 EUR    EUR Bank
             100 PHP    PHP Bank
            5481 PHP    USD Bank
--------------------
             100 EUR
            5581 PHP
</pre></div>

<p>The latest available price is used.  The syntax
<samp class="option">-X <var class="var">COMMODITY1</var>:<var class="var">COMMODITY2</var></samp> displays values in <var class="var">COMMODITY1</var>
in terms of <var class="var">COMMODITY2</var> using the latest available price, but
will not automatically convert any other commodities to
<var class="var">COMMODITY2</var>.  Multiple <samp class="option">-X</samp> arguments may be used on a
single command-line (as in
<samp class="option">-X COMMODITY1:COMMODITY2 -X COMMODITY3:COMMODITY2</samp>),
which is particularly useful for situations where many prices are
available for reporting in terms of <var class="var">COMMODITY2</var>, but only a few
should be displayed that way.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dflat'><span><samp class="option">--flat</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dflat'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Force the full names of accounts to be used in the balance report.  The
balance report will not use an indented tree.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dforce_002dcolor'><span><samp class="option">--force-color</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dforce_002dcolor'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Output TTY color codes even if the TTY doesn&rsquo;t support them.  Useful
for TTYs that don&rsquo;t advertise their capabilities correctly.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dforce_002dpager'><span><samp class="option">--force-pager</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dforce_002dpager'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Force Ledger to paginate its output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dforecast_002dwhile-VEXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">--forecast-while <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dforecast_002dwhile-VEXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dforecast-VEXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">--forecast <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dforecast-VEXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Continue forecasting while <var class="var">VEXPR</var> is true.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dforecast_002dyears-INT'><span><samp class="option">--forecast-years <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dforecast_002dyears-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Forecast at most <var class="var">INT</var> years into the future.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dF-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">-F <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dF-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use the given format string to print output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dgain-1'><span><samp class="option">--gain</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dgain-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dG-1'><span><samp class="option">-G</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dG-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dchange'><span><samp class="option">--change</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dchange'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report on gains using the latest available prices.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dgenerated'><span><samp class="option">--generated</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dgenerated'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Include auto-generated postings (such as those from automated
transactions) in the report, in cases where you normally wouldn&rsquo;t want
them.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dgroup_002dby-EXPR'><span><samp class="option">--group-by <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dgroup_002dby-EXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Group transactions together in the <code class="command">register</code> report.
<var class="var">EXPR</var> can be anything, although most common would be <code class="code">payee</code>
or <code class="code">commodity</code>.  The <code class="code">tags()</code> function is also useful here.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dgroup_002dtitle_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--group-title-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dgroup_002dtitle_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format for the headers that separates the report sections of
a grouped report.  Only has an effect with a <samp class="option">--group-by
<var class="var">EXPR</var></samp> register report.
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger reg Expenses --group-by &quot;payee&quot; --group-title-format &quot;------------------------ %-20(value) ---------------------\n&quot;
</pre></div>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">------------------------ 7-Eleven             ---------------------
2011/08/13 7-Eleven              Expenses:Auto:Misc          $ 5.80       $ 5.80

------------------------ AAA Dues             ---------------------
2011/06/02 AAA Dues              Expenses:Auto:Misc        $ 215.00     $ 215.00

------------------------ ABC Towing and Wrecking ---------------------
2011/03/17 ABC Towing and Wrec..  Expenses:Auto:Hobbies      $ 48.20      $ 48.20
...
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dhead-INT-1'><span><samp class="option">--head <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dhead-INT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dfirst-INT'><span><samp class="option">--first <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dfirst-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Print the first <var class="var">INT</var> entries.  Opposite of <samp class="option">--tail
<var class="var">INT</var></samp>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dhistorical'><span><samp class="option">--historical</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dhistorical'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dH'><span><samp class="option">-H</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dH'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Value commodities at the time of their acquisition.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dimmediate-1'><span><samp class="option">--immediate</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dimmediate-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Evaluate calculations immediately rather than lazily.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dinject'><span><samp class="option">--inject</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dinject'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use <code class="code">Expected</code> amounts in calculations.  In case you know
what amount a transaction should be, but the actual transaction has the
wrong value you can use metadata to specify the expected amount:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">2012-03-12  Paycheck
    Income  $-990;  Expected:: $-1000.00
    Checking
</pre></div>

<p>Then using the command <code class="code">ledger reg --inject=Expected Income</code> would
treat the transaction as if the &ldquo;Expected Value&rdquo; was actual.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dinvert-1'><span><samp class="option">--invert</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dinvert-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Change the sign of all reported values.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlimit-EXPR-3'><span><samp class="option">--limit <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlimit-EXPR-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dl-EXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">-l <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dl-EXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Only transactions that satisfy <var class="var">EXPR</var> are considered in
calculations and for display.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlot_002ddates-1'><span><samp class="option">--lot-dates</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlot_002ddates-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the date on which each commodity in a balance report was
purchased.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlot_002dnotes-1'><span><samp class="option">--lot-notes</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlot_002dnotes-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlot_002dtags'><span><samp class="option">--lot-tags</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlot_002dtags'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the tag attached to each commodity in a balance report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlot_002dprices-1'><span><samp class="option">--lot-prices</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlot_002dprices-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the price at which each commodity in a balance report was
purchased.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlots-1'><span><samp class="option">--lots</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlots-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the date and price at which each commodity was purchased in
a balance report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlots_002dactual'><span><samp class="option">--lots-actual</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlots_002dactual'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Preserve the uniqueness of commodities so they aren&rsquo;t merged during
reporting without printing the lot annotations.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmarket-4'><span><samp class="option">--market</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmarket-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dV-1'><span><samp class="option">-V</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dV-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use the latest market value for all commodities.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmeta-TAG'><span><samp class="option">--meta <var class="var">TAG</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmeta-TAG'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>In the register report, prepend the transaction with the value of the
given <var class="var">TAG</var>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmeta_002dwidth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--meta-width <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmeta_002dwidth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the width of the Meta column used for the <samp class="option">--meta
<var class="var">TAG</var></samp> options.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmonthly-3'><span><samp class="option">--monthly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmonthly-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dM-1'><span><samp class="option">-M</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dM-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Synonym for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--period &quot;monthly&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002daliases-1'><span><samp class="option">--no-aliases</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002daliases-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Aliases are completely ignored.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002dcolor'><span><samp class="option">--no-color</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002dcolor'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Suppress any color TTY output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002dpager-1'><span><samp class="option">--no-pager</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002dpager-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Direct output to stdout, avoiding pager program.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002drevalued'><span><samp class="option">--no-revalued</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002drevalued'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Stop Ledger from showing <code class="code">&lt;Revalued&gt;</code> postings.  This option is useful
in combination with the <samp class="option">--exchange</samp> or <samp class="option">--market</samp> option.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002drounding'><span><samp class="option">--no-rounding</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002drounding'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Don&rsquo;t output &lsquo;<samp class="samp">&lt;Adjustment&gt;</samp>&rsquo; postings.  Note that this will cause the
running total to often not add up!  Its main use is for
<samp class="option">--amount-data (-j)</samp> and <samp class="option">--total-data (-J)</samp> reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002dtitles'><span><samp class="option">--no-titles</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002dtitles'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Suppress the output of group titles.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002dtotal'><span><samp class="option">--no-total</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002dtotal'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Suppress printing the final total line in a balance report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dnow-DATE'><span><samp class="option">--now <var class="var">DATE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dnow-DATE'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define the current date in case you want to calculate in the past or
future using <samp class="option">--current</samp>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002donly-FIXME'><span><samp class="option">--only <var class="var">FIXME</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002donly-FIXME'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>This is a postings predicate that applies after certain transforms have
been executed, such as periodic gathering.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002doutput-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">--output <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002doutput-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Redirect the output of ledger to the file defined in <samp class="file">FILE</samp>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpager-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">--pager <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpager-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Direct output to <var class="var">FILE</var> pager program.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpayee-VEXPR'><span><samp class="option">--payee <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpayee-VEXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Sets a value expression for formatting the payee.  In the
<code class="command">register</code> report this prevents the second entry from having
a date and payee for each transaction.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpayee_002dwidth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--payee-width <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpayee_002dwidth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the number of columns dedicated to the payee in the register
report to <var class="var">INT</var>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpending-1'><span><samp class="option">--pending</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpending-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use only postings that are marked pending.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpercent-1'><span><samp class="option">--percent</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpercent-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_0025-1'><span><samp class="option">-%</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_0025-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Calculate the percentage value of each account in balance reports.
Only works for accounts that have a single commodity.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dperiod-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-1'><span><samp class="option">--period <var class="var">PERIOD_EXPRESSION</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dperiod-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define a period expression that sets the time period during which
transactions are to be accounted.  For a <code class="command">register</code> report only
the transactions that satisfy the period expression with be displayed.
For a <code class="command">balance</code> report only those transactions will be accounted
in the final balances.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpivot-TAG-1'><span><samp class="option">--pivot <var class="var">TAG</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpivot-TAG-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Produce a balance pivot report <em class="emph">around</em> the given <var class="var">TAG</var>.  For
example, if you have multiple cars and track each fuel purchase in
&lsquo;<samp class="samp">Expenses:Auto:Fuel</samp>&rsquo; and tag each fuel purchase with a tag
identifying which car the purchase was for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">; Car: Prius</samp>&rsquo;, then the
command:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger bal Fuel --pivot &quot;Car&quot; --period &quot;this year&quot;
</pre></div>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">           $ 3491.26  Car
           $ 1084.22    M3:Expenses:Auto:Fuel
            $ 149.65    MG V11:Expenses:Auto:Fuel
            $ 621.89    Prius:Expenses:Auto:Fuel
           $ 1635.50    Sienna:Expenses:Auto:Fuel
             $ 42.69  Expenses:Auto:Fuel
--------------------
           $ 3533.95
</pre></div>

<p>See <a class="xref" href="#Metadata-values">Metadata values</a>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dplot_002damount_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--plot-amount-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dplot_002damount_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define the output format for an amount data plot.  See <a class="xref" href="#Visualizing-with-Gnuplot">Visualizing with Gnuplot</a>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dplot_002dtotal_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--plot-total-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dplot_002dtotal_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define the output format for a total data plot.  See <a class="xref" href="#Visualizing-with-Gnuplot">Visualizing with Gnuplot</a>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprepend_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--prepend-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprepend_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Prepend <var class="var">STR</var> to every line of the output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprepend_002dwidth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--prepend-width <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprepend_002dwidth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Reserve <var class="var">INT</var> spaces at the beginning of each line of the output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprice'><span><samp class="option">--price</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprice'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dI'><span><samp class="option">-I</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dI'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use the price of the commodity purchase for performing calculations.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpricedb_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'><span><samp class="option">--pricedb-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpricedb_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format expected for the historical price file.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprices_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--prices-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprices_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format for the <code class="command">prices</code> report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprimary_002ddate'><span><samp class="option">--primary-date</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprimary_002ddate'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dactual_002ddates'><span><samp class="option">--actual-dates</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dactual_002ddates'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show primary dates for all calculations (see <a class="pxref" href="#Effective-Dates">Effective Dates</a>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dquantity-1'><span><samp class="option">--quantity</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dquantity-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dO-1'><span><samp class="option">-O</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dO-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report commodity totals (this is the default).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dquarterly-2'><span><samp class="option">--quarterly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dquarterly-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Synonym for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--period &quot;quarterly&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002draw'><span><samp class="option">--raw</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002draw'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>In the <code class="command">print</code> report, show transactions using the exact same
syntax as specified by the user in their data file.  Don&rsquo;t do any
massaging or interpreting.  This can be useful for minor cleanups, like
just aligning amounts.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dreal-3'><span><samp class="option">--real</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dreal-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dR-1'><span><samp class="option">-R</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Account using only real transactions ignoring virtual and automatic
transactions.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dregister_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--register-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dregister_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define the output format for the <code class="command">register</code> report.
</p>
</dd>
