<dt id='index-_002d_002drelated-2'><span><samp class="option">--related</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drelated-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>In a <code class="command">register</code> report show the related account.  This is the
other <em class="emph">side</em> of the transaction.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002drelated_002dall'><span><samp class="option">--related-all</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drelated_002dall'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show all postings in a transaction, similar to <samp class="option">--related</samp> but
show both <em class="emph">sides</em> of each transaction.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002drevalued'><span><samp class="option">--revalued</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drevalued'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report discrepancy in values for manual reports by inserting <code class="code">&lt;Revalued&gt;</code>
postings.  This is implied when using the <samp class="option">--exchange</samp> or
<samp class="option">--market</samp> option.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002drevalued_002donly'><span><samp class="option">--revalued-only</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drevalued_002donly'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show only <code class="code">&lt;Revalued&gt;</code> postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002drevalued_002dtotal-FIXME'><span><samp class="option">--revalued-total <var class="var">FIXME</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drevalued_002dtotal-FIXME'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display the sum of the revalued postings as the running total, which serves
to show unrealized capital in a gain/losses report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002drich_002ddata-1'><span><samp class="option">--rich-data</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drich_002ddata-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddetail'><span><samp class="option">--detail</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddetail'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>When generating a ledger transaction from a CSV file using the
<code class="command">convert</code> command, add CSV, Imported, and UUID metadata.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dseed-INT'><span><samp class="option">--seed <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dseed-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the random seed to <var class="var">INT</var> for the <code class="code">generate</code> command.
Used as part of development testing.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsort-VEXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">--sort <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsort-VEXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dS-VEXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">-S <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dS-VEXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Sort the <code class="command">register</code> report based on the value expression given
to sort.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsort_002dall-FIXME'><span><samp class="option">--sort-all <var class="var">FIXME</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsort_002dall-FIXME'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p><small class="sc">UNDOCUMENTED</small>! Please help by contributing documentation for this feature.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsort_002dxacts-VEXPR'><span><samp class="option">--sort-xacts <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsort_002dxacts-VEXPR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dperiod_002dsort-VEXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">--period-sort <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dperiod_002dsort-VEXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Sort the postings within transactions using the given value expression.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dstart_002dof_002dweek-INT'><span><samp class="option">--start-of-week <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dstart_002dof_002dweek-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Tell ledger to use a particular day of the week to start its &ldquo;weekly&rdquo;
summary.  &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--start-of-week=1</samp>&rsquo; specifies Monday as the start of the
week.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsubtotal-4'><span><samp class="option">--subtotal</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsubtotal-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002ds-2'><span><samp class="option">-s</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002ds-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Cause all transactions in a <code class="command">register</code> report to be collapsed
into a single, subtotaled transaction.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtail-INT-1'><span><samp class="option">--tail <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtail-INT-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlast-INT'><span><samp class="option">--last <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlast-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report only the last <var class="var">INT</var> entries.  Only useful in
a <code class="command">register</code> report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtime_002dreport'><span><samp class="option">--time-report</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtime_002dreport'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Add two columns to the balance report to show the earliest checkin and
checkout times for timelog entries.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtotal-VEXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">--total <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtotal-VEXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dT-VEXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">-T <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dT-VEXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define a value expression used to calculate the total in reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtotal_002ddata-3'><span><samp class="option">--total-data</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtotal_002ddata-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dJ-1'><span><samp class="option">-J</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dJ-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show only dates and totals to format the output for plots.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtotal_002dwidth-INT'><span><samp class="option">--total-width <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtotal_002dwidth-INT'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the width of the total field in the register report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtruncate-CODE'><span><samp class="option">--truncate <var class="var">CODE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtruncate-CODE'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Indicates how truncation should happen when the contents of columns
exceed their width.  Valid arguments are &lsquo;<samp class="samp">leading</samp>&rsquo;, &lsquo;<samp class="samp">middle</samp>&rsquo;,
and &lsquo;<samp class="samp">trailing</samp>&rsquo;.  The default is smarter than any of these three,
as it considers sub-names within the account name (that style is
called &ldquo;abbreviate&rdquo;).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dunbudgeted-1'><span><samp class="option">--unbudgeted</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dunbudgeted-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show only unbudgeted postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002duncleared-2'><span><samp class="option">--uncleared</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002duncleared-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dU-1'><span><samp class="option">-U</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dU-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use only uncleared transactions in calculations and reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dunrealized'><span><samp class="option">--unrealized</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dunrealized'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show generated unrealized gain and loss accounts in the balance
report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dunrealized_002dgains-STR'><span><samp class="option">--unrealized-gains <var class="var">STR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dunrealized_002dgains-STR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Allow the user to specify what account name should be used for
unrealized gains.  Defaults to &lsquo;<samp class="samp">&quot;Equity:Unrealized Gains&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
Often set in one&rsquo;s init file to change the default.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dunrealized_002dlosses-STR'><span><samp class="option">--unrealized-losses <var class="var">STR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dunrealized_002dlosses-STR'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Allow the user to specify what account name should be used for
unrealized losses.  Defaults to &lsquo;<samp class="samp">&quot;Equity:Unrealized Losses&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
Often set in one&rsquo;s init file to change the default.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dunround'><span><samp class="option">--unround</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dunround'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Perform all calculations without rounding and display results to full
precision.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dvalues-1'><span><samp class="option">--values</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dvalues-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Shows the values used by each tag when used in combination with the
<code class="command">tags</code> command.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dweekly-2'><span><samp class="option">--weekly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dweekly-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dW-2'><span><samp class="option">-W</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dW-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Synonym for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--period &quot;weekly&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dwide-1'><span><samp class="option">--wide</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dwide-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Let the register report use 132 columns instead of 80 (the default).
Identical to &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--columns &quot;132&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dyearly-2'><span><samp class="option">--yearly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dyearly-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dY-2'><span><samp class="option">-Y</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dY-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Synonym for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">--period &quot;yearly&quot;</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Basic-options">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Report-filtering" accesskey="n" rel="next">Report filtering</a>, Previous: <a href="#Report-Options" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Report Options</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Basic-options-1">8.3.4 Basic options</h4>

<p>These are the most basic command options.  Most likely, the user will
want to set them using environment variables (see <a class="ref" href="#Environment-variables">Environment variables</a>), instead of using actual command-line options:
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dhelp-2'><span><samp class="option">--help</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dhelp-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dh-2'><span><samp class="option">-h</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dh-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display the man page for <samp class="file">ledger</samp>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dversion-2'><span><samp class="option">--version</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dversion-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Print the current version of ledger and exits.  This is useful for
sending bug reports, to let the author know which version of ledger you
are using.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dfile-FILE-2'><span><samp class="option">--file <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dfile-FILE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002df-FILE-2'><span><samp class="option">-f <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002df-FILE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Read <samp class="file">FILE</samp> as a ledger file.  <var class="var">FILE</var> can be &lsquo;<samp class="samp">-</samp>&rsquo; which is
a synonym for &lsquo;<samp class="samp">/dev/stdin</samp>&rsquo;.  This command may be used multiple
times.  Typically, the environment variable <code class="env">LEDGER_FILE</code> is set,
rather than using this command-line option.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002doutput-FILE-2'><span><samp class="option">--output <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002doutput-FILE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002do-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">-o <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002do-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Redirect output from any command to <samp class="file">FILE</samp>.  By default, all output
goes to standard output.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dinit_002dfile-FILE-2'><span><samp class="option">--init-file <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dinit_002dfile-FILE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002di-FILE-1'><span><samp class="option">-i <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002di-FILE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Causes <samp class="file">FILE</samp> to be read by ledger before any other ledger file.
This file may not contain any postings, but it may contain option
settings.  To specify options in the init file, use the same syntax as
on the command-line, but put each option on its own line.  Here is an
example init file:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">--price-db ~/finance/.pricedb
--wide
; ~/.ledgerrc ends here
</pre></div>

<p>Option settings on the command-line or in the environment always take
precedence over settings in the init file.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daccount-STR-3'><span><samp class="option">--account <var class="var">STR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daccount-STR-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002da-STR-1'><span><samp class="option">-a <var class="var">STR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002da-STR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Specify the default account which QIF file postings are assumed to
relate to.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Report-filtering">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Output-customization" accesskey="n" rel="next">Output customization</a>, Previous: <a href="#Basic-options" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Basic options</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Report-filtering-1">8.3.5 Report filtering</h4>

<p>These options change which postings affect the outcome of a
report, in ways other than just using regular expressions:
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcurrent-2'><span><samp class="option">--current</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcurrent-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dc-1'><span><samp class="option">-c</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dc-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display only transactions occurring on or before the current date.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbegin-DATE-2'><span><samp class="option">--begin <var class="var">DATE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbegin-DATE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002db-DATE-1'><span><samp class="option">-b <var class="var">DATE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002db-DATE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Constrain the report to transactions on or after <var class="var">DATE</var>.  Only
transactions after that date will be calculated, which means that the
running total in the balance report will always start at zero with the
first matching transaction.  (Note: This is different from using
<samp class="option">--display <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp> to constrain what is displayed).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dend-DATE-2'><span><samp class="option">--end <var class="var">DATE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dend-DATE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002de-DATE-1'><span><samp class="option">-e <var class="var">DATE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002de-DATE-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Constrain the report so that transactions on or after <var class="var">DATE</var> are
not considered.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dperiod-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-2'><span><samp class="option">--period <var class="var">PERIOD_EXPRESSION</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dperiod-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dp-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-1'><span><samp class="option">-p <var class="var">PERIOD_EXPRESSION</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dp-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the reporting period to <var class="var">STR</var>.  This will subtotal all matching
transactions within each period separately, making it easy to see
weekly, monthly, quarterly, etc., posting totals.  A period string can
even specify the beginning and end of the report range, using simple
terms like &lsquo;<samp class="samp">last June</samp>&rsquo; or &lsquo;<samp class="samp">next month</samp>&rsquo;.  For more details on
period expressions, see <a class="ref" href="#Period-Expressions">Period Expressions</a>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dperiod_002dsort-VEXPR-3'><span><samp class="option">--period-sort <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dperiod_002dsort-VEXPR-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Sort the postings within each reporting period using the value
expression <var class="var">EXPR</var>.  This is most often useful when reporting
monthly expenses, in order to view the highest expense categories at
the top of each month:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -M --period-sort total reg ^Expenses
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcleared-3'><span><samp class="option">--cleared</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcleared-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dC-2'><span><samp class="option">-C</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dC-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display only postings whose transaction has been marked &ldquo;cleared&rdquo;
(by placing an asterisk to the right of the date).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002duncleared-3'><span><samp class="option">--uncleared</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002duncleared-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dU-2'><span><samp class="option">-U</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dU-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display only postings whose transaction has not been marked &ldquo;cleared&rdquo;
(i.e., if there is no asterisk to the right of the date).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dreal-4'><span><samp class="option">--real</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dreal-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dR-2'><span><samp class="option">-R</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display only real postings, not virtual.  (A virtual posting is
indicated by surrounding the account name with parentheses or brackets;
see <a class="ref" href="#Virtual-postings">Virtual postings</a> for more information).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dactual-2'><span><samp class="option">--actual</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dactual-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dL-2'><span><samp class="option">-L</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dL-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display only actual postings, and not those created by automated
transactions.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002drelated-3'><span><samp class="option">--related</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002drelated-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dr-1'><span><samp class="option">-r</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dr-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Display postings that are related to whichever postings would
otherwise have matched the filtering criteria.  In the register
report, this shows where money went to, or the account it came from.
In the balance report, it shows all the accounts affected by
transactions having a related posting.  For example, if a file had
this transaction:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">2004/03/20 Safeway
    Expenses:Food                       $65.00
    Expenses:Cash                       $20.00
    Assets:Checking                    $-85.00
</pre></div>

<p>And the register command was:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -f example.dat -r register food
</pre></div>

<p>The following would be printed, showing the postings related to the
posting that matched:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">04-Mar-20 Safeway               Expenses:Cash                $20.00       $20.00
                                Assets:Checking             $-85.00      $-65.00
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbudget-3'><span><samp class="option">--budget</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbudget-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Useful for displaying how close your postings meet your budget.
<samp class="option">--add-budget</samp> also shows unbudgeted postings, while
<samp class="option">--unbudgeted</samp> shows only those.  <samp class="option">--forecast <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp>
is a related option that projects your budget into the future, showing
how it will affect future balances.  See <a class="xref" href="#Budgeting-and-Forecasting">Budgeting and Forecasting</a>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dlimit-EXPR-4'><span><samp class="option">--limit <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dlimit-EXPR-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dl-EXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">-l <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dl-EXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Limit which postings take part in the calculations of a report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002damount-EXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">--amount <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002damount-EXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dt-EXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">-t <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dt-EXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Change the value expression used to calculate the &ldquo;value&rdquo; column in
the <code class="command">register</code> report, the amount used to calculate account
totals in the <code class="command">balance</code> report, and the values printed in the
<code class="command">equity</code> report.  See <a class="xref" href="#Value-Expressions">Value Expressions</a>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtotal-VEXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">--total <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtotal-VEXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dT-VEXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">-T <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dT-VEXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the value expression used for the &ldquo;totals&rdquo; column in the
<code class="command">register</code> and <code class="command">balance</code> reports.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>







<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Output-customization">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Commodity-reporting" accesskey="n" rel="next">Commodity reporting</a>, Previous: <a href="#Report-filtering" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Report filtering</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Output-customization-1">8.3.6 Output customization</h4>

<p>These options affect only the output, but not which postings are
used to create it:
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcollapse-2'><span><samp class="option">--collapse</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcollapse-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dn-2'><span><samp class="option">-n</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dn-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Cause transactions in a <code class="command">register</code> report with multiple
postings to be collapsed into a single, subtotaled transaction.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsubtotal-5'><span><samp class="option">--subtotal</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsubtotal-5'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002ds-3'><span><samp class="option">-s</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002ds-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Cause all transactions in a <code class="command">register</code> report to be collapsed
into a single, subtotaled transaction.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dby_002dpayee-5'><span><samp class="option">--by-payee</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dby_002dpayee-5'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dP-3'><span><samp class="option">-P</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dP-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report subtotals by payee.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dempty-3'><span><samp class="option">--empty</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dempty-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dE-2'><span><samp class="option">-E</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Include even empty accounts in the <code class="command">balance</code> report.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dweekly-3'><span><samp class="option">--weekly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dweekly-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dW-3'><span><samp class="option">-W</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dW-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals by the week.  The week begins on whichever day of
the week begins the month containing that posting.  To set a specific
begin date, use a period string, such as &lsquo;<samp class="samp">weekly from DATE</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmonthly-4'><span><samp class="option">--monthly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmonthly-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dM-2'><span><samp class="option">-M</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dM-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals by month.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dyearly-3'><span><samp class="option">--yearly</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dyearly-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dY-3'><span><samp class="option">-Y</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dY-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals by year.  For more complex periods, use
<samp class="option">--period</samp>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dperiod-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-3'><span><samp class="option">--period <var class="var">PERIOD_EXPRESSION</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dperiod-PERIOD_005fEXPRESSION-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Option described above.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddow-3'><span><samp class="option">--dow</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddow-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report posting totals for each day of the week.  This is an easy way
to see if weekend spending is more than on weekdays.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dsort-VEXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">--sort <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dsort-VEXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dS-VEXPR-2'><span><samp class="option">-S <var class="var">VEXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dS-VEXPR-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Sort a report by comparing the values determined using the value
expression <var class="var">VEXPR</var>.  For example, using &lsquo;<samp class="samp">-S &quot;-abs(total)&quot;</samp>&rsquo; in
the <code class="command">balance</code> report will sort account balances from greatest to
least, using the absolute value of the total.  For more on how to use
value expressions, see <a class="ref" href="#Value-Expressions">Value Expressions</a>.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpivot-TAG-2'><span><samp class="option">--pivot <var class="var">TAG</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpivot-TAG-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Produce a pivot table around the <var class="var">TAG</var> provided.  This requires
meta data using valued tags.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dwide-2'><span><samp class="option">--wide</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dwide-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dw-1'><span><samp class="option">-w</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dw-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Cause the default <code class="command">register</code> report to assume 132 columns
instead of 80.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dhead-INT-2'><span><samp class="option">--head <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dhead-INT-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Cause only the first <var class="var">INT</var> transactions to be printed.  This is
different from using the command-line utility <samp class="file">head</samp>, which would
limit to the first <var class="var">INT</var> postings.  <samp class="option">--tail <var class="var">INT</var></samp> outputs
only the last <var class="var">INT</var> transactions.  Both options may be used
simultaneously.  If a negative amount is given, it will invert the
meaning of the flag (instead of the first five transactions being
printed, for example, it would print all but the first five).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpager-FILE-2'><span><samp class="option">--pager <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpager-FILE-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Tell Ledger to pass its output to the given <var class="var">FILE</var> pager program;
very useful when the output is especially long.  This behavior can be
made the default by setting the <code class="env">LEDGER_PAGER</code> environment variable.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dno_002dpager-2'><span><samp class="option">--no-pager</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dno_002dpager-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Tell Ledger to <em class="emph">not</em> pass its output to a pager program; useful
when a pager is set by default.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002daverage-3'><span><samp class="option">--average</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002daverage-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dA-2'><span><samp class="option">-A</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dA-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the average posting value.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddeviation-2'><span><samp class="option">--deviation</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddeviation-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dD-3'><span><samp class="option">-D</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dD-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report each posting&rsquo;s deviation from the average.  It is only meaningful
in the <code class="command">register</code> and <code class="command">prices</code> reports.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpercent-2'><span><samp class="option">--percent</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpercent-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_0025-2'><span><samp class="option">-%</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_0025-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Show account subtotals in the <code class="command">balance</code> report as percentages of
the parent account.
</p>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002damount_002ddata-4'><span><samp class="option">--amount-data</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002damount_002ddata-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dj-2'><span><samp class="option">-j</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dj-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Change the <code class="command">register</code> report so that it prints nothing but the
date and the value column, and the latter without commodities.  This is
only meaningful if the report uses a single commodity.  This data can
then be fed to other programs, which could plot the date, analyze it,
etc.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dtotal_002ddata-4'><span><samp class="option">--total-data</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dtotal_002ddata-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dJ-2'><span><samp class="option">-J</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dJ-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Change the <code class="command">register</code> report so that it prints nothing but the
date and total columns, without commodities.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddisplay-EXPR-4'><span><samp class="option">--display <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddisplay-EXPR-4'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dd-EXPR-1'><span><samp class="option">-d <var class="var">EXPR</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dd-EXPR-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Limit which postings or accounts are actually displayed in a report.
They might still be calculated, and be part of the running total of a
register report, for example, but they will not be displayed.  This is
useful for seeing last month&rsquo;s checking postings, against a running
balance which includes all posting values:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -d &quot;d&gt;=[last month]&quot; reg checking
</pre></div>

<p>The output from this command is very different from the following,
whose running total includes only postings from the last month
onward:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -p &quot;last month&quot; reg checking
</pre></div>

<p>Which is more useful depends on what you&rsquo;re looking to know: the total
amount for the reporting range (using <samp class="option">--period
<var class="var">PERIOD_EXPRESSION</var> (-p)</samp>), or simply a display restricted to the
reporting range (using <samp class="option">--display <var class="var">EXPR</var> (-d)</samp>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT-2'><span><samp class="option">--date-format <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddate_002dformat-DATE_005fFORMAT-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dy-DATE_005fFORMAT-2'><span><samp class="option">-y <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dy-DATE_005fFORMAT-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Change the basic date format used by reports.  The default uses a date
like &lsquo;<samp class="samp">2004/08/01</samp>&rsquo;, which represents the default date format of
<code class="code">%Y/%m/%d</code>.  To change the way dates are printed in general, the
easiest way is to put <samp class="option">--date-format <var class="var">DATE_FORMAT</var></samp> in the
Ledger init file (or the file referred to by <code class="env">LEDGER_INIT</code>).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'><span><samp class="option">--format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dF-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'><span><samp class="option">-F <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dF-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the reporting format for whatever report ledger is about to make.
See <a class="xref" href="#Format-Strings">Format Strings</a>.  There are also specific format commands for
each report type:
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbalance_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'><span><samp class="option">--balance-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbalance_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define the output format for the <code class="command">balance</code> report.  The default
(defined in <samp class="file">report.h</samp> is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(ansify_if(
        justify(scrub(display_total), 20,
                20 + int(prepend_width), true, color),
                  bold if should_bold))
        %(!options.flat ? depth_spacer : \&quot;\&quot;)
      %-(ansify_if(
         ansify_if(partial_account(options.flat), blue if color),
                   bold if should_bold))\n%/
      %$1\n%/
      %(prepend_width ? \&quot; \&quot; * int(prepend_width) : \&quot;\&quot;)
      --------------------\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcleared_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--cleared-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcleared_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define the format for the cleared report.  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(justify(scrub(get_at(display_total, 0)), 16, 16 + int(prepend_width),
       true, color))  %(justify(scrub(get_at(display_total, 1)), 18,
       36 + int(prepend_width), true, color))
          %(latest_cleared ? format_date(latest_cleared) : \&quot;         \&quot;)
          %(!options.flat ? depth_spacer : \&quot;\&quot;)
      %-(ansify_if(partial_account(options.flat), blue if color))\n%/
      %$1  %$2    %$3\n%/
      %(prepend_width ? \&quot; \&quot; * int(prepend_width) : \&quot;\&quot;)
      ----------------    ----------------    ---------\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dregister_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'><span><samp class="option">--register-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dregister_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Define the output format for the <code class="command">register</code> report.  The default
(defined in <samp class="file">report.h</samp> is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(ansify_if(
        ansify_if(justify(format_date(date), int(date_width)),
                  green if color and date &gt; today),
                  bold if should_bold))
       %(ansify_if(
         ansify_if(justify(truncated(payee, int(payee_width)), int(payee_width)),
                   bold if color and !cleared and actual),
                   bold if should_bold))
       %(ansify_if(
         ansify_if(justify(truncated(display_account, int(account_width),
                                     int(abbrev_len)), int(account_width)),
                   blue if color),
                   bold if should_bold))
       %(ansify_if(
         justify(scrub(display_amount), int(amount_width),
                 3 + int(meta_width) + int(date_width) + int(payee_width)
                   + int(account_width) + int(amount_width) + int(prepend_width),
                 true, color),
                 bold if should_bold))
       %(ansify_if(
         justify(scrub(display_total), int(total_width),
                 4 + int(meta_width) + int(date_width) + int(payee_width)
                   + int(account_width) + int(amount_width) + int(total_width)
                   + int(prepend_width), true, color),
                 bold if should_bold))\n%/
      %(justify(\&quot; \&quot;, int(date_width)))
       %(ansify_if(
         justify(truncated(has_tag(\&quot;Payee\&quot;) ? payee : \&quot; \&quot;,
                           int(payee_width)), int(payee_width)),
                   bold if should_bold))
       %$3 %$4 %$5\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dcsv_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--csv-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dcsv_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format for <code class="command">csv</code> reports.  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(quoted(date)),
 %(quoted(code)),
 %(quoted(payee)),
 %(quoted(display_account)),
 %(quoted(commodity(scrub(display_amount)))),
 %(quoted(quantity(scrub(display_amount)))),
 %(quoted(cleared ? \&quot;*\&quot; : (pending ? \&quot;!\&quot; : \&quot;\&quot;))),
 %(quoted(join(note | xact.note)))\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dplot_002damount_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'><span><samp class="option">--plot-amount-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dplot_002damount_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format for amount plots, using the <samp class="option">--amount-data (-j)</samp>
option.  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(format_date(date, \&quot;%Y-%m-%d\&quot;)) %(quantity(scrub(display_amount)))\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dplot_002dtotal_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'><span><samp class="option">--plot-total-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dplot_002dtotal_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format for total plots, using the <samp class="option">--total-data (-J)</samp>
option.  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(format_date(date, \&quot;%Y-%m-%d\&quot;)) %(quantity(scrub(display_total)))\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dpricedb_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'><span><samp class="option">--pricedb-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dpricedb_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-1'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format expected for the historical price file.  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;P %(datetime) %(display_account) %(scrub(display_amount))\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprices_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'><span><samp class="option">--prices-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprices_002dformat-FORMAT_005fSTRING-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the format for the <code class="command">prices</code> report.  The default is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&quot;%(date) %-8(display_account) %(justify(scrub(display_amount), 12,
           2 + 9 + 8 + 12, true, color))\n&quot;
</pre></div>

</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Commodity-reporting">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Environment-variables" accesskey="n" rel="next">Environment variables</a>, Previous: <a href="#Output-customization" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Output customization</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Commodity-reporting-1">8.3.7 Commodity reporting</h4>

<p>These options affect how commodity values are displayed:
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprice_002ddb-FILE-3'><span><samp class="option">--price-db <var class="var">FILE</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprice_002ddb-FILE-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the file that is used for recording downloaded commodity prices.
It is always read on startup, to determine historical prices.  Other
settings can be placed in this file manually, to prevent downloading
quotes for a specific commodity, for example.  This is done by adding a
line like the following:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">; Don't download quotes for the dollar, or timelog values
N $
N h
</pre></div>

<p>Note: Ledger NEVER writes output to files.  You are responsible for
updating the price-db file.  The best way is to have your price
download script maintain this file.
</p>
<p>The format of the file can be changed by telling ledger to use the
<samp class="option">--pricedb-format <var class="var">FORMAT_STRING</var></samp> you define.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dprice_002dexp-INT-2'><span><samp class="option">--price-exp <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dprice_002dexp-INT-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dleeway-INT-2'><span><samp class="option">--leeway <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dleeway-INT-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dZ-INT-2'><span><samp class="option">-Z <var class="var">INT</var></samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dZ-INT-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Set the expected freshness of price quotes, in <var class="var">INT</var> minutes.  That
is, if the last known quote for any commodity is older than this value,
and if <samp class="option">--download</samp> is being used, then the Internet will be
consulted again for a newer price.  Otherwise, the old price is still
considered to be fresh enough.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002ddownload-3'><span><samp class="option">--download</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002ddownload-3'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dQ-2'><span><samp class="option">-Q</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dQ-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Cause quotes to be automagically downloaded, as needed, by running
a script named <samp class="file">getquote</samp> and expecting that script to return
a value understood by ledger.  A sample implementation of
a <samp class="file">getquote</samp> script, implemented in Perl, is provided in the
distribution.  Downloaded quote price are then appended to the price
database, usually specified using the environment variable
<code class="env">LEDGER_PRICE_DB</code>.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<p>There are several different ways that ledger can report the totals it
displays.  The most flexible way to adjust them is by using value
expressions, and the <samp class="option">--amount <var class="var">EXPR</var> (-t)</samp> and
<samp class="option">--total <var class="var">VEXPR</var> (-T)</samp> options.  However, there are also
several &ldquo;default&rdquo; reports, which will satisfy most users&rsquo; basic
reporting needs:
</p>
<dl class="ftable">
<dt id='index-_002d_002dquantity-2'><span><samp class="option">--quantity</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dquantity-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dO-2'><span><samp class="option">-O</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dO-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report commodity totals (this is the default).
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dbasis-2'><span><samp class="option">--basis</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dbasis-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dB-2'><span><samp class="option">-B</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dB-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the cost basis for all postings.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dmarket-5'><span><samp class="option">--market</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dmarket-5'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dV-2'><span><samp class="option">-V</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dV-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Use the last known value for commodities to calculate final values.
</p>
</dd>
<dt id='index-_002d_002dgain-2'><span><samp class="option">--gain</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002d_002dgain-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dt id='index-_002dG-2'><span><samp class="option">-G</samp><a class="copiable-link" href='#index-_002dG-2'> &para;</a></span></dt>
<dd><p>Report the net gain/loss for all commodities in the report that have
a price history.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<p>Often you will be more interested in the value of your entire holdings,
in your preferred currency.  It might be nice to know you hold 10,000
shares of PENNY, but you are more interested in whether or not that is
worth $1000.00 or $10,000.00.  However, the current day value of a
commodity can mean different things to different people, depending on
the accounts involved, the commodities, the nature of the transactions,
etc.
</p>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dnow-DATE-1"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dmarket-6"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dexchange-_0022COMMODITY-_005b_002c-COMMODITY_002c-_002e_002e_002e_005d_0022-3"></a>

<p>When you specify <samp class="option">--market (-V)</samp>, or <samp class="option">--exchange
<var class="var">COMMODITY</var> (-X)</samp>, you are requesting that some or all of the
commodities be valuated as of today (or whatever <samp class="option">--now
<var class="var">DATE</var></samp> is set to).  But what does such a valuation mean? This
meaning is governed by the presence of a <var class="var">VALUE</var> meta-data property,
whose content is an expression used to compute that value.
</p>
<p>If no <var class="var">VALUE</var> property is specified, each posting is assumed to have
a default, as if you&rsquo;d specified a global, automated transaction as
follows:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">= expr true
    ; VALUE:: market(amount, date, exchange)
</pre></div>

<p>This definition emulates the present day behavior of <samp class="option">--market
(-V)</samp> and <samp class="option">--exchange <var class="var">COMMODITY</var> (-X)</samp> (in the case of
&lsquo;<samp class="samp">-X</samp>&rsquo;, the requested commodity is passed via the string
&lsquo;<samp class="samp">exchange</samp>&rsquo; above).
</p>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-Euro-conversion"></a>
<p>One thing many people have wanted to do is to fixate the valuation of
old European currencies in terms of the Euro after a certain date:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">= expr commodity == &quot;DM&quot;
    ; VALUE:: date &lt; [Jun 2008] ? market(amount, date, exchange) : 1.44 EUR
</pre></div>

<p>This says: If <samp class="option">--now <var class="var">DATE</var></samp> is some old date, use market
prices as they were at that time; but if <samp class="option">--now <var class="var">DATE</var></samp> is
past June 2008, use a fixed price for converting Deutsche Mark to Euro.
</p>
<p>Or how about never re-valuating commodities used in Expenses, since
they cannot have a different future value:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">= /^Expenses:/
    ; VALUE:: market(amount, post.date, exchange)
</pre></div>

<p>This says the future valuation is the same as the valuation at the time
of posting.  <code class="code">post.date</code> equals the posting&rsquo;s date, while just &rsquo;date&rsquo; is
the value of <samp class="option">--now <var class="var">DATE</var></samp> (defaults to today).
</p>
<p>Or how about valuating miles based on a reimbursement rate during a
specific time period:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">= expr commodity == &quot;miles&quot; and date &gt;= [2007] and date &lt; [2008]
    ; VALUE:: market($1.05, date, exchange)
</pre></div>

<p>In this case, miles driven in 2007 will always be valuated at $1.05
each.  If you use &lsquo;<samp class="samp">-X EUR</samp>&rsquo; to expressly request all amounts in
Euro, Ledger shall convert $1.05 to Euro by whatever means are
appropriate for dollars.
</p>
<p>Note that you can have a valuation expression specific to a particular
posting or transaction, by overriding these general defaults using
specific meta-data:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">2010-12-26 Example
    Expenses:Food                $20
    ; Just to be silly, always valuate *these* $20 as 30 DM, no matter what
    ; the user asks for with -V or -X
    ; VALUE:: 30 DM
    Assets:Cash
</pre></div>

<p>This example demonstrates that your value expression should be as
symbolic as possible, using terms like &rsquo;amount&rsquo; and &rsquo;date&rsquo;, rather than
specific amounts and dates.  Also, you should pass the amount along to
the function &rsquo;market&rsquo; so it can be further revalued if the user has
asked for a specific currency.
</p>
<p>Or, if it better suits your accounting, you can be less symbolic,
which allows you to report most everything in EUR if you use &lsquo;<samp class="samp">-X
EUR</samp>&rsquo;, except for certain accounts or postings which should always be
valuated in another currency.  For example:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">= /^Assets:Brokerage:CAD$/
    ; Always report the value of commodities in this account in
    ; terms of present day dollars, despite what was asked for
    ; on the command-line VALUE:: market(amount, date, &lsquo;<samp class="samp">$</samp>&rsquo;)
</pre></div>

<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-FIFO_002fLIFO"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-LIFO_002fFIFO"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dlots-2"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dlot_002dprices-2"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dexchange-_0022COMMODITY-_005b_002c-COMMODITY_002c-_002e_002e_002e_005d_0022-4"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dhistorical-1"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dbasis-3"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dprice-1"></a>

<p>Ledger presently has no way of handling such things as FIFO and LIFO.
</p>
<p>If you specify an unadorned commodity name, like AAPL, it will balance
against itself.  If <samp class="option">--lots</samp> are not being displayed, then it
will appear to balance against any lot of AAPL.
</p>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-adorned-commodity"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dlot_002dprices-3"></a>
<p>If you specify an adorned commodity, like AAPL {$10.00}, it will also
balance against itself, and against any AAPL if <samp class="option">--lots</samp> is not
specified.  But if you do specify <samp class="option">--lot-prices</samp>, for example,
then it will balance against that specific price for AAPL.
</p>
<p>Normally when you use <samp class="option">--exchange <var class="var">COMMODITY</var> (-X)</samp> to
request that amounts be reported in a specific commodity, Ledger uses
these values:
</p>
<ul class="itemize mark-bullet">
<li>Register Report
For the <code class="command">register</code> report, use the value of that commodity on
the date of the posting being reported, with a &lsquo;<samp class="samp">&lt;Revalued&gt;</samp>&rsquo; posting
added at the end if today&rsquo;s value is different from the value of the
last posting.

</li><li>Balance Report
For the <code class="command">balance</code> report, use the value of that commodity as of
today.

</li></ul>

<p>You can now specify <samp class="option">--historical (-H)</samp> to ask that all
valuations for any amount be done relative to the date that amount was
encountered.
</p>
<p>You can also now use <samp class="option">--exchange <var class="var">COMMODITY</var> (-X)</samp> (and
<samp class="option">--historical (-H)</samp>) in conjunction with <samp class="option">--basis (-B)</samp>
and <samp class="option">--price (-I)</samp>, to see valuation reports of just your basis
costs or lot prices.
</p>
<p>Finally, sometimes, you may seek to only report one (or some subset) of
the commodities in terms of another commodity.  In this situation, you
can use the syntax <samp class="option">--exchange <var class="var">COMMODITY1</var>:<var class="var">COMMODITY2</var></samp>
to request that ledger always display <var class="var">COMMODITY1</var> in terms of
<var class="var">COMMODITY2</var>, but you want no other commodities to be automatically
displayed in terms of <var class="var">COMMODITY2</var> without additional
<samp class="option">--exchange</samp> options.  For example, if you wanted to report EUR
and BTC in terms of USD, but report all other commodities without
conversion to USD, you could use: <samp class="option">--exchange EUR:USD --exchange
BTC:USD</samp>.
</p>
<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Environment-variables">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Previous: <a href="#Commodity-reporting" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Commodity reporting</a>, Up: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="u" rel="up">Detailed Option Description</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Environment-variables-1">8.3.8 Environment variables</h4>

<p>Every option to ledger may be set using an environment variable if the
option has a long name.  For example setting the environment variable
&lsquo;<samp class="samp"><code class="env">LEDGER_DATE_FORMAT</code>=&quot;%d.%m.%Y&quot;</samp>&rsquo; will have the same effect as specifying
&lsquo;<samp class="samp"><samp class="option">--date-format</samp> '%d.%m.%Y'</samp>&rsquo; on the command-line.  Options on the
command-line always take precedence over environment variable settings, however.
</p>
<p>Note that you may also permanently specify option values by placing
option settings in the file <samp class="file">~/.ledgerrc</samp> one option per line, for example:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">--pager /bin/cat
--date-format %d.%m.%Y
</pre></div>

<hr>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section-level-extent" id="Period-Expressions">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Previous: <a href="#Detailed-Option-Description" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Detailed Option Description</a>, Up: <a href="#Command_002dLine-Syntax" accesskey="u" rel="up">Command-Line Syntax</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h3 class="section" id="Period-Expressions-1">8.4 Period Expressions</h3>

<p>A period expression indicates a span of time, or a reporting interval,
or both. Ledger&rsquo;s end dates are always exclusive, imagine the date is
followed by 00:00:00 time. They are instants in time not entire days.
The full syntax is:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">[INTERVAL] [BEGIN] [END]
</pre></div>

<p>The optional <var class="var">INTERVAL</var> part may be any one of:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">every day
every week
every month
every quarter
every year
every N days     # N is any integer
every N weeks
every N months
every N quarters
every N years
daily
weekly
biweekly
monthly
bimonthly
quarterly
yearly
</pre></div>

<p>After the interval, a begin time, end time, both or neither may be
specified.  As for the begin time, it can be either of:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">from &lt;SPEC&gt;
since &lt;SPEC&gt;
</pre></div>

<p>The end time can be either of:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">to &lt;SPEC&gt;
until &lt;SPEC&gt;
</pre></div>

<p>Where <var class="var">SPEC</var> can be any of:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">2004
2004/10
2004/10/1
10/1
october
oct
this week  # or day, month, quarter, year
next week
last week
</pre></div>

<p>The beginning and ending can be given at the same time, if it spans a
single period.  In that case, just use <var class="var">SPEC</var> by itself.  In that
case, the period &lsquo;<samp class="samp">oct</samp>&rsquo;, for example, will cover all the days in
October.  The possible forms are:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">&lt;SPEC&gt;
in &lt;SPEC&gt;
</pre></div>

<p>Here are a few examples of period expressions:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">monthly
monthly in 2004
weekly from oct
weekly from last month
from sep to oct
from 10/1 to 10/5
monthly until 2005
from apr
until nov
last oct
weekly last august
</pre></div>

<hr>
</div>
</div>
<div class="chapter-level-extent" id="Budgeting-and-Forecasting">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Time-Keeping" accesskey="n" rel="next">Time Keeping</a>, Previous: <a href="#Command_002dLine-Syntax" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Command-Line Syntax</a>, Up: <a href="#Top" accesskey="u" rel="up">Overview</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h2 class="chapter" id="Budgeting-and-Forecasting-1">9 Budgeting and Forecasting</h2>


<ul class="mini-toc">
<li><a href="#Budgeting" accesskey="1">Budgeting</a></li>
<li><a href="#Forecasting" accesskey="2">Forecasting</a></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="section-level-extent" id="Budgeting">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Forecasting" accesskey="n" rel="next">Forecasting</a>, Previous: <a href="#Budgeting-and-Forecasting" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Budgeting and Forecasting</a>, Up: <a href="#Budgeting-and-Forecasting" accesskey="u" rel="up">Budgeting and Forecasting</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h3 class="section" id="Budgeting-1">9.1 Budgeting</h3>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dbudget-4"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dadd_002dbudget-2"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dunbudgeted-2"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dmonthly-5"></a>

<p>Keeping a budget allows you to pay closer attention to your income and
expenses, by reporting how far your actual financial activity is from
your expectations.
</p>
<p>To start keeping a budget, put some periodic transactions
(see <a class="pxref" href="#Periodic-Transactions">Periodic Transactions</a>) at the top of your ledger file.  A
periodic transaction is almost identical to a regular transaction, except
that it begins with a tilde and has a period expression in place of a
payee.  For example:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">~ Monthly
    Expenses:Rent               $500.00
    Expenses:Food               $450.00
    Expenses:Auto:Gas           $120.00
    Expenses:Insurance          $150.00
    Expenses:Phone              $125.00
    Expenses:Utilities          $100.00
    Expenses:Movies              $50.00
    Expenses                    $200.00  ; all other expenses
    Assets

~ Yearly
    Expenses:Auto:Repair        $500.00
    Assets
</pre></div>

<p>These two periodic transactions give the usual monthly expenses, as well
as one typical yearly expense.  For help on finding out what your
average monthly expenses are for any category, use a command like:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -p &quot;this year&quot; --monthly --average register ^expenses
</pre></div>

<p>The reported totals are the current year&rsquo;s average for each account.
</p>
<p>Once these periodic transactions are defined, creating a budget report is
as easy as adding <samp class="option">--budget</samp> to the command-line.  For example,
a typical monthly expense report would be:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger --monthly register ^expenses
</pre></div>

<p>To see the same report balanced against your budget, use:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger --budget --monthly register ^expenses
</pre></div>

<p>A budget report includes only those accounts that appear in the budget.
To see all expenses balanced against the budget, use
<samp class="option">--add-budget</samp>.  You can even see only the unbudgeted expenses
using <samp class="option">--unbudgeted</samp>:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger --unbudgeted --monthly register ^expenses
</pre></div>

<p>You can also use these flags with the <code class="command">balance</code> command.
</p>
<hr>
</div>
<div class="section-level-extent" id="Forecasting">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Previous: <a href="#Budgeting" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Budgeting</a>, Up: <a href="#Budgeting-and-Forecasting" accesskey="u" rel="up">Budgeting and Forecasting</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h3 class="section" id="Forecasting-1">9.2 Forecasting</h3>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dforecast-VEXPR-2"></a>

<p>Sometimes it&rsquo;s useful to know what your finances will look like in the
future, such as determining when an account will reach zero.  Ledger
makes this easy to do, using the same periodic transactions as are used
for budgeting.  An example forecast report can be generated with:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger --file drewr3.dat --forecast &quot;T&gt;{\$-500.00}&quot; register ^assets ^liabilities
</pre></div>

<p>This report continues outputting postings until the running total
is greater than $-500.00.  A final posting is always shown, to
inform you what the total afterwards would be.
</p>
<p>Forecasting can also be used with the <code class="command">balance</code> report,
but by date only, and not against the running total:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger --forecast &quot;d&lt;[2010]&quot; bal ^assets ^liabilities
</pre></div>

<hr>
</div>
</div>
<div class="chapter-level-extent" id="Time-Keeping">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Value-Expressions" accesskey="n" rel="next">Value Expressions</a>, Previous: <a href="#Budgeting-and-Forecasting" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Budgeting and Forecasting</a>, Up: <a href="#Top" accesskey="u" rel="up">Overview</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h2 class="chapter" id="Time-Keeping-1">10 Time Keeping</h2>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dday_002dbreak-1"></a>

<a class="anchor" id="timelog"></a><p>Ledger directly supports &ldquo;timelog&rdquo; entries, which have this form:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">i 2013/03/28 22:13:00 ACCOUNT[  PAYEE]
o 2013/03/29 03:39:00
</pre></div>

<p>This records a check-in to the given ACCOUNT, and a check-out.  You can
be checked-in to multiple accounts at a time, if you wish, and they can
span multiple days (use <samp class="option">--day-break</samp> to break them up in the
report).  The number of seconds between check-in and check-out is
accumulated as time to that ACCOUNT.  If the checkout uses a capital
&lsquo;<samp class="samp">O</samp>&rsquo;, the transaction is marked &ldquo;cleared&rdquo;.  You can use an
optional PAYEE for whatever meaning you like.
</p>
<p>Now, there are a few ways to generate this information.  You can use
the <samp class="file">timeclock.el</samp> package, which is part of Emacs.  Or you can
write a simple script in whichever language you prefer to emit similar
information.  Or you can use Org mode&rsquo;s time-clocking abilities and
the <samp class="file">org2tc</samp> script developed by John Wiegley.
</p>
<p>These timelog entries can appear in a separate file, or directly in
your main ledger file.  The initial &lsquo;<samp class="samp">i</samp>&rsquo; and &lsquo;<samp class="samp">o</samp>&rsquo; characters
count as Ledger &ldquo;directives&rdquo;, and are accepted anywhere that
ordinary transactions are valid.
</p>
<hr>
</div>
<div class="chapter-level-extent" id="Value-Expressions">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Format-Strings" accesskey="n" rel="next">Format Strings</a>, Previous: <a href="#Time-Keeping" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Time Keeping</a>, Up: <a href="#Top" accesskey="u" rel="up">Overview</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h2 class="chapter" id="Value-Expressions-1">11 Value Expressions</h2>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dlimit-EXPR-5"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002ddisplay-EXPR-5"></a>

<p>Ledger uses value expressions to make calculations for many different
purposes:
</p>
<ol class="enumerate">
<li> The values displayed in reports.

</li><li> For predicates (where truth is anything non-zero), to determine which
postings are calculated (option <samp class="option">--limit <var class="var">EXPR</var> (-l)</samp>) or
displayed (option <samp class="option">--display <var class="var">EXPR</var> (-d)</samp>).

</li><li> For sorting criteria, to yield the sort key.

</li><li> In the matching criteria used by automated postings.

</li></ol>

<p>Value expressions support most simple math and logic operators, in
addition to a set of functions and variables.
</p>



<p>Display predicates are also very handy with register reports, to
constrain which transactions are printed.  For example, the following
command shows only transactions from the beginning of the current month,
while still calculating the running balance based on all transactions:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -d &quot;d&gt;[this month]&quot; register checking
</pre></div>

<p>The advantage of this command&rsquo;s complexity is that it prints the
running total in terms of all transactions in the register.  The
following, simpler command is similar, but totals only the displayed
postings:
</p>
<div class="example smallexample">
<pre class="example-preformatted">$ ledger -b &quot;this month&quot; register checking
</pre></div>


<ul class="mini-toc">
<li><a href="#Variables" accesskey="1">Variables</a></li>
<li><a href="#Functions" accesskey="2">Functions</a></li>
<li><a href="#Operators" accesskey="3">Operators</a></li>
<li><a href="#Complex-expressions" accesskey="4">Complex expressions</a></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="section-level-extent" id="Variables">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Functions" accesskey="n" rel="next">Functions</a>, Previous: <a href="#Value-Expressions" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Value Expressions</a>, Up: <a href="#Value-Expressions" accesskey="u" rel="up">Value Expressions</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h3 class="section" id="Variables-1">11.1 Variables</h3>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002damount-EXPR-3"></a>
<a class="index-entry-id" id="index-_002d_002dtotal-VEXPR-3"></a>

<p>Below are the one letter variables available in any value expression.
For the <code class="command">register</code> and <code class="command">print</code> commands, these variables
relate to individual postings, and sometimes the account affected by a
posting.  For the <code class="command">balance</code> command, these variables relate to
accounts, often with a subtle difference in meaning.  The use of each
variable for both is specified.
</p>
<dl class="table">
<dt><code class="code">t</code></dt>
<dd><p>This maps to whatever the user specified with <samp class="option">--amount
<var class="var">EXPR</var> (-t)</samp>.  In a <code class="command">register</code> report, <samp class="option">--amount
<var class="var">EXPR</var> (-t)</samp> changes the value column; in a <code class="command">balance</code>
report, it has no meaning by default.  If <samp class="option">--amount <var class="var">EXPR</var>
(-t)</samp> was not specified, the current report style&rsquo;s value expression is
used.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">T</code></dt>
<dd><p>This maps to whatever the user specified with <samp class="option">--total
<var class="var">VEXPR</var> (-T)</samp>.  In a register report, <samp class="option">--total <var class="var">VEXPR</var>
(-T)</samp> changes the totals column; in a balance report, this is the value
given for each account.  If <samp class="option">--total <var class="var">VEXPR</var> (-T)</samp> was not
specified, the current report style&rsquo;s value expression is used.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">m</code></dt>
<dd><p>This is always the present moment/date.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>


<ul class="mini-toc">
<li><a href="#Posting_002faccount-details" accesskey="1">Posting/account details</a></li>
<li><a href="#Calculated-totals" accesskey="2">Calculated totals</a></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Posting_002faccount-details">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Calculated-totals" accesskey="n" rel="next">Calculated totals</a>, Previous: <a href="#Variables" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Variables</a>, Up: <a href="#Variables" accesskey="u" rel="up">Variables</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Posting_002faccount-details-1">11.1.1 Posting/account details</h4>

<dl class="table">
<dt><code class="code">d</code></dt>
<dt><code class="code">date</code></dt>
<dd><p>A posting&rsquo;s date, as the number of seconds past the epoch.  This
is always &ldquo;today&rdquo; for an account.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">aux_date</code></dt>
<dd><p>A posting&rsquo;s aux date
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">a</code></dt>
<dt><code class="code">amount</code></dt>
<dd><p>The posting&rsquo;s amount; the balance of an account, without
considering children.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">b</code></dt>
<dd><p>The cost of a posting; the cost of an account, without its
children.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">v</code></dt>
<dd><p>The market value of a posting or an account, without its children.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">g</code></dt>
<dd><p>The net gain (market value minus cost basis), for a posting or an
account, without its children.  It is the same as &lsquo;<samp class="samp">v-b</samp>&rsquo;.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">depth</code></dt>
<dd><p>The depth (&ldquo;level&rdquo;) of an account.  If an account has one parent,
its depth is one.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">n</code></dt>
<dd><p>The index of a posting, or the count of postings affecting an
account.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">X</code></dt>
<dt><code class="code">cleared</code></dt>
<dd><p>&lsquo;<samp class="samp">1</samp>&rsquo; if a posting&rsquo;s transaction has been cleared, &lsquo;<samp class="samp">0</samp>&rsquo; otherwise.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">uncleared</code></dt>
<dd><p>&lsquo;<samp class="samp">1</samp>&rsquo; if a posting&rsquo;s transaction state is uncleared, &lsquo;<samp class="samp">0</samp>&rsquo; otherwise.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">pending</code></dt>
<dd><p>&lsquo;<samp class="samp">1</samp>&rsquo; if a posting&rsquo;s transaction state is pending, &lsquo;<samp class="samp">0</samp>&rsquo; otherwise.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">R</code></dt>
<dd><p>&lsquo;<samp class="samp">1</samp>&rsquo; if a posting is not virtual, &lsquo;<samp class="samp">0</samp>&rsquo; otherwise.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">Z</code></dt>
<dd><p>&lsquo;<samp class="samp">1</samp>&rsquo; if a posting is not automated, &lsquo;<samp class="samp">0</samp>&rsquo; otherwise.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
<div class="subsection-level-extent" id="Calculated-totals">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Previous: <a href="#Posting_002faccount-details" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Posting/account details</a>, Up: <a href="#Variables" accesskey="u" rel="up">Variables</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h4 class="subsection" id="Calculated-totals-1">11.1.2 Calculated totals</h4>

<dl class="table">
<dt><code class="code">O</code></dt>
<dd><p>The total of all postings seen so far, or the total of an account
and all its children.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">N</code></dt>
<dd><p>The total count of postings affecting an account and all its
children.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
</div>
<div class="section-level-extent" id="Functions">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>
Next: <a href="#Operators" accesskey="n" rel="next">Operators</a>, Previous: <a href="#Variables" accesskey="p" rel="prev">Variables</a>, Up: <a href="#Value-Expressions" accesskey="u" rel="up">Value Expressions</a> &nbsp; [<a href="#SEC_Contents" title="Table of contents" rel="contents">Contents</a>][<a href="#Concepts-Index" title="Index" rel="index">Index</a>]</p>
</div>
<h3 class="section" id="Functions-1">11.2 Functions</h3>

<p>The available one letter functions are:
</p>
<dl class="table">
<dt><code class="code">-</code></dt>
<dd><p>Negates the argument.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">U</code></dt>
<dd><p>The absolute (unsigned) value of the argument.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">S</code></dt>
<dd><p>Strips the commodity from the argument.
</p>
</dd>
<dt><code class="code">P</code></dt>
<dd><p>The present market value of the argument.  The syntax &lsquo;<samp class="samp">P(x,d)</samp>&rsquo; is
supported, which yields the market value at time &lsquo;<samp class="samp">d</samp>&rsquo;.  If no date
is given, then the current moment is used.
</p>
</dd>
</dl>

<hr>
</div>
<div class="section-level-extent" id="Operators">
<div class="nav-panel">
<p>

<h3 class="section" id="Operators-1">11.3 Operators</h3>

<p>The operators, in order of precedence, are:
</p>
<ol class="enumerate">
<li> <code class="code">* /</code>
</li><li> <code class="code">+ -</code>
</li><li> <code class="code">! &lt; &gt; =</code>
</li><li> <code class="code">&amp; | ?:</code>
</li></ol>
